<ul data-start="725" data-end="837">
<li data-start="725" data-end="774">
<p data-start="727" data-end="774">Search for <strong data-start="738" data-end="757"><code data-start="740" data-end="755">hanysabeh.dev</code></strong> and register it.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="775" data-end="837">
<p data-start="777" data-end="837">Youâ€™ll need to provide your name, email, and payment method.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="839" data-end="842">
<h4 data-start="844" data-end="874"><strong data-start="849" data-end="874">2. Create the Website</strong></h4>
<p data-start="876" data-end="934">You have 3 main options depending on your skills and time:</p>
<h5 data-start="936" data-end="1002">ðŸŸ¢ Option A: Use GitHub + Free Hosting (Best for Developers)</h5>
<ul data-start="1003" data-end="1270">
<li data-start="1003" data-end="1058">
<p data-start="1005" data-end="1058">Create an account at <a data-start="1026" data-end="1058" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://github.com/">github.com</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1059" data-end="1109">
<p data-start="1061" data-end="1109">Create a repository called <code data-start="1088" data-end="1109">hanysabeh.github.io</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1110" data-end="1227">
<p data-start="1112" data-end="1227">Upload your HTML files (or use a site generator like <a data-start="1165" data-end="1196" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://jekyllrb.com/">Jekyll</a> or <a data-start="1200" data-end="1226" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://gohugo.io/">Hugo</a>)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1228" data-end="1270">
<p data-start="1230" data-end="1270">Set up GitHub Pages in the repo Settings</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1272" data-end="1340">âž¡ï¸ Then, <strong data-start="1281" data-end="1307">link the custom domain</strong> <code data-start="1308" data-end="1323">hanysabeh.dev</code> to GitHub Pages:</p>
<ul data-start="1341" data-end="1495">
<li data-start="1341" data-end="1403">
<p data-start="1343" data-end="1403">Add a <code data-start="1349" data-end="1356">CNAME</code> file in the repo with content: <code data-start="1388" data-end="1403">hanysabeh.dev</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1404" data-end="1495">
<p data-start="1406" data-end="1495">In your domain provider, add a DNS <code data-start="1441" data-end="1444">A</code> record pointing to GitHubâ€™s servers (or use CNAME)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 data-start="1497" data-end="1559">ðŸŸ  Option B: Use a No-Code Website Builder (Fastest Way)</h5>
<p data-start="1560" data-end="1564">Use:</p>
<ul data-start="1565" data-end="1725">
<li data-start="1565" data-end="1593">
<p data-start="1567" data-end="1593"><a data-start="1567" data-end="1593" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://www.wix.com/">Wix</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1594" data-end="1630">
<p data-start="1596" data-end="1630"><a data-start="1596" data-end="1630" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://www.webflow.com/">Webflow</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1631" data-end="1682">
<p data-start="1633" data-end="1682"><a data-start="1633" data-end="1658" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://carrd.co/">Carrd</a> (simple and very cheap)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1683" data-end="1725">
<p data-start="1685" data-end="1725"><a data-start="1685" data-end="1725" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://sites.google.com/">Google Sites</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1727" data-end="1756">Design the site easily, then:</p>
<ul data-start="1757" data-end="1838">
<li data-start="1757" data-end="1838">
<p data-start="1759" data-end="1838">Connect your custom domain <code data-start="1786" data-end="1801">hanysabeh.dev</code> inside the builder's domain settings</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 data-start="1840" data-end="1896">ðŸ”µ Option C: Deploy from Code (Flask/Django/React)</h5>
<ul data-start="1897" data-end="2130">
<li data-start="1897" data-end="1961">
<p data-start="1899" data-end="1961">Create a portfolio with Python (Flask or Django) or JS (React)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1962" data-end="2070">
<p data-start="1964" data-end="2070">Deploy it on <a data-start="1977" data-end="2005" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://vercel.com/">Vercel</a>, <a data-start="2007" data-end="2037" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://netlify.com/">Netlify</a>, or <a data-start="2042" data-end="2070" class="" rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://render.com/">Render</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2071" data-end="2130">
<p data-start="2073" data-end="2130">Use your domain settings to point to the hosting platform</p>
</li>
</ul>

<p data-start="2276" data-end="2305">ðŸ“Š Projects with GitHub links</p>
</li>

<p data-start="2308" data-end="2326">ðŸ§  Blog (optional)</p>

<p data-start="2329" data-end="2352">ðŸ“ž Contact info or form</p>
